Style Change Notification Phase\\nWhen CSS properties change (via class/attribute changes, inline style modifications, or stylesheet updates), RestyleManager::PostRestyleEvent (layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp:2383) is called to queue style recalculation. This function posts the element for restyle processing.\\n\\n### 2. Flush Pending Notifications\\nWhen the page needs to be laid out or painted, PresShell::DoFlushPendingNotifications (layout/base/PresShell.cpp:4357) is invoked. This function orchestrates the complete flush sequence by:\\n- Calling RestyleManager::ProcessPendingRestyles (layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp:3284)\\n- Then calling PresShell::DoFlushLayout (layout/base/PresShell.cpp:10716) which invokes ProcessReflowCommands\\n\\n### 3. Style Recomputation\\nRestyleManager::ProcessPendingRestyles (layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp:3284) delegates to DoProcessPendingRestyles (layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp:3087), which uses the Servo style engine to recompute styles for invalidated elements. This results in updated ComputedStyle objects being attached to elements.\\n\\n### 4. Frame Style Application\\nOnce styles are recomputed, nsIFrame::DidSetComputedStyle (layout/generic/nsIFrame.cpp:1240) is called for each affected frame.
